(a) the relative ranking of certain indebtedness of the Debtors;

(b) the relative ranking of certain security granted by the Debtors;

(c) when payments can be made in respect of certain indebtedness of the Debtors;

(d) when enforcement actions can be taken in respect of that indebtedness;
